<Rating>5< /Rating><pics>None< /pics><userid>114090303610107282873<//userid>< text>
We were having dinner across the street when I noticed Reed and Greenough. I asked our server if he recommended it, he said definitely,  and I'm glad he did. It's a very comfortable, laid back feeling inside. Everyone in our group is our 60's but never felt out of place amongst the mostly 30 something's that make up most of the clientele. We made this our last stop of the night for 4 out of the 5 days we were in San Francisco. Look to see if the piano bar sign is lit up outside so u'll know if one of the 2 guys that play piano and sing are ther that night. They were both great! Having gone 4 nights , the bartenders greeted us by name when we walked in, which of course made us feel even more welcome. The drinks were great and avg price for the area but it was the friendly relaxed, even on sat night when it was crowed,atmosphere that kept us coming back. Up front is the bar and intimate seating along the wall, further back a pool table, if you want to play. Our bartenders were Dan,Ernie and taking orders from the seating area was Rafael.  The were all extremely friendly and make a great drink. Go, enjoy and have one for me !< /text>
